\noindent230 (all 552) SAMBs

\vspace{5mm}

\noindent\textbullet\, '\texttt{A}' site-cluster

\noindent\quad * bra: $\bra{\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{1}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},\frac{3}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{3}{2};p}$

\noindent\quad * ket: $\ket{\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{1}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},\frac{3}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{3}{2};p}$

\noindent\quad * wyckoff: \texttt{8b}

\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z1}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(c)}(A_{g},a)=\mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(a)}(A_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(s)}(A_{g})
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z2}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(c)}(A_{g},b)=\frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3}
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z3}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(1,-1;c)}(A_{g})=\frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(s)}(T_{g})}{3}
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z4}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(1,1;c)}(A_{g})=\mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(1,1;a)}(A_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(s)}(A_{g})
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z5}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{3}^{(c)}(A_{u},a)=\mathbb{Q}_{0}^{(a)}(A_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{3}^{(s)}(A_{u})
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z27}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{3}^{(c)}(A_{u},b)=\frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,1}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,2}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,3}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3}
\end{dmath*}
\begin{dmath*}
\fbox{z28}\quad \mathbb{Q}_{3}^{(1,-1;c)}(A_{u})=\frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,1}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,1}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,2}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,2}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3} + \frac{\sqrt{3} \mathbb{Q}_{2,3}^{(1,-1;a)}(T_{g}) \mathbb{Q}_{1,3}^{(s)}(T_{u})}{3}

\noindent\textbullet\, '\texttt{A}'-'\texttt{A}' bond-cluster

\noindent\quad * bra: $\bra{\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{1}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},\frac{3}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \bra{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{3}{2};p}$

\noindent\quad * ket: $\ket{\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{1}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},\frac{3}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},\frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{1}{2};p},\, \ket{\frac{3}{2},- \frac{3}{2};p}$

\noindent\quad * wyckoff: \texttt{12b@12c}
